\u003ccode\u003escTenifoldNet()\u003c/code\u003e function orchestrates a six-step pipeline. Each step reports progress to the console via the \u003ca href=\"https://cli.r-lib.org/\" rel=\"nofollow\"\u003ecli\u003c/a\u003e package, with sample-level labels (\u003ccode\u003e[X]\u003c/code\u003e / \u003ccode\u003e[Y]\u003c/code\u003e) so that operations on each condition are clearly distinguishable.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cmarkdown-accessiblity-table\u003e\u003ctable\u003e\n\u003cthead\u003e\n\u003ctr\u003e\n\u003cth align=\"center\"\u003eStep\u003c/th\u003e\n\u003cth align=\"center\"\u003e1\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd align=\"left\"\u003e\u003ccode\u003escQC\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd align=\"left\"\u003eQuality control — filters cells by library size, outlier detection, minimum gene expression fraction, and mitochondrial read ratio\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003c/tr\u003e\n\u003ctr\u003e\n\u003ctd align=\"center\"\u003e2\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd normalization\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003c/tr\u003e\n\u003ctr\u003e\n\u003ctd align=\"center\"\u003e3\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd align=\"left\"\u003e\u003ccode\u003emakeNetworks\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd align=\"left\"\u003eConstructs gene regulatory networks from subsampled cells using principal component regression (\u003ccode\u003epcNet\u003c/code\u003e)\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003c/tr\u003e\n\u003ctr\u003e\n\u003ctd align=\"center\"\u003e4\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd statistics\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003c/tr\u003e\n\u003c/tbody\u003e\n\u003c/table\u003e\u003c/markdown-accessiblity-table\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eIndividual functions are exported and fully regulatory networks after CP tensor decomposition, containing:\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003eX\u003c/code\u003e: The network for sample \u003cem\u003eX\u003c/em\u003e (sparse matrix of class \u003ccode\u003edgCMatrix\u003c/code\u003e).\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003eY\u003c/code\u003e: The network for sample \u003cem\u003eY\u003c/em\u003e (sparse data frame of low-dimensional features from the non-linear manifold alignment, with 2 × \u003cem\u003en\u003c/em\u003e genes rows and \u003cem\u003ed\u003c/em\u003e columns (default \u003cem\u003ed\u003c/em\u003e = 30).\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003e\u003ccode\u003ediffRegulation\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/strong\u003e — A data frame with six columns:\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003egene\u003c/code\u003e: Gene identifier.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003edistance\u003c/code\u003e: Euclidean distance between the gene's coordinates in the two conditions.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003eZ\u003c/code\u003e: Z-score after Box-Cox power transformation.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003eFC\u003c/code\u003e: Fold change with respect to the expectation.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003ep.value\u003c/code\u003e: P-value from the chi-square distribution with one degree of freedom.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003ep.adj\u003c/code\u003e: Adjusted p-value (Benjamini \u0026amp; Hochberg FDR correction).\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch2 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" scTenifoldNet","","[![CRAN](https://www.r-pkg.org/badges/version/scTenifoldNet)](https://CRAN.R-project.org/package=scTenifoldNet)","[![License: GPL (\u003e=2)](https://img.shields.io/badge/License-GPL%20%28%3E%3D2%29-blue.svg)](https://www.gnu.org/licenses/old-licenses/gpl-2.0.en.html)","","**scTenifoldNet** is an R package for constructing and comparing single-cell gene regulatory networks (scGRNs) from single-cell RNA-seq (scRNA-seq) data collected under different conditions. It employs a machine-learning workflow combining principal component regression, tensor decomposition, and manifold alignment to accurately identify even subtly shifted gene expression programs.","","Implementations in other languages are also available:","","- **Python**: [scTenifoldpy](https://github.com/qwerty239qwe/scTenifoldpy)","- **MATLAB**: [scGEAToolbox](https://github.com/jamesjcai/scGEAToolbox)","","## Installation","","**scTenifoldNet** is available on CRAN:","","```r","install.packages(\"scTenifoldNet\")","```","","To install the development version from GitHub:","","```r","# install.packages(\"remotes\")","remotes::install_github(\"cailab-tamu/scTenifoldNet\")","```","","## Pipeline Overview","","The `scTenifoldNet()` function orchestrates a six-step pipeline. Each step reports progress to the console via the [cli](https://cli.r-lib.org/) package, with sample-level labels (`[X]` / `[Y]`) so that operations on each condition are clearly distinguishable.","","| Step | Function | Description |","|:----:|:---------|:------------|","| 1 | `scQC` | Quality control — filters cells by library size, outlier detection, minimum gene expression fraction, and mitochondrial read ratio |","| 2 | `cpmNormalization` | Counts-per-million (CPM) normalization |","| 3 | `makeNetworks` | Constructs gene regulatory networks from subsampled cells using principal component regression (`pcNet`) |","| 4 | `tensorDecomposition` | CANDECOMP/PARAFAC (CP) tensor decomposition for network denoising |","| 5 | `manifoldAlignment` | Non-linear manifold alignment of the two denoised networks |","| 6 | `dRegulation` | Differential regulation testing via Box-Cox transformation and chi-square statistics |","","Individual functions are exported and fully documented, allowing users to run or modify any step independently.","","## Input","","The required input is a **raw counts matrix** with genes as rows and cells (barcodes) as columns. Data should be *unnormalized* when using the main `scTenifoldNet()` function. The modular design of the package allows users to substitute custom preprocessing at any step.","","## Output","","`scTenifoldNet()` returns a list with three elements:","","- **`tensorNetworks`** — Weight-averaged denoised gene regulatory networks after CP tensor decomposition, containing:","  - `X`: The network for sample *X* (sparse matrix of class `dgCMatrix`).","  - `Y`: The network for sample *Y* (sparse matrix of class `dgCMatrix`).","- **`manifoldAlignment`** — A data frame of low-dimensional features from the non-linear manifold alignment, with 2 × *n* genes rows and *d* columns (default *d* = 30).","- **`diffRegulation`** — A data frame with six columns:","  - `gene`: Gene identifier.","  - `distance`: Euclidean distance between the gene's coordinates in the two conditions.","  - `Z`: Z-score after Box-Cox power transformation.","  - `FC`: Fold change with respect to the expectation.","  - `p.value`: P-value from the chi-square distribution with one degree of freedom.","  - `p.adj`: Adjusted p-value (Benjamini \u0026 Hochberg FDR correction).","","## Running Time","","Running time is largely determined by the network construction step and scales with the number of cells and genes. Representative benchmarks:","","| Cells | Genes | Time | Memory |","|------:|------:|-----:|-------:|","| 300 | 1,000 | 3.5 min | 0.4 GB |","| 1,000 | 1,000 | 4.3 min | 0.4 GB |","| 1,000 | 5,000 | 2 h 52 min | 9.2 GB |","| 2,500 | 5,000 | 2 h 55 min | 9.5 GB |","| 5,000 | 5,000 | 3 h 9 min | 10.1 GB |","| 5,000 | 7,500 | 3 h 10 min | 21.8 GB |","| 7,500 | 5,000 | 10 h 16 min | 10.6 GB |","| 7,500 | 7,500 | 10 h 16 min | 22.6 GB |","","## Example","","### Simulating a dataset","","We create a sparse count matrix of 2,000 cells and 100 genes drawn from a negative binomial distribution (~67 % zeros). The last ten genes are prefixed with `mt-` to simulate mitochondrial genes.","","```r","library(scTenifoldNet)","","nCells \u003c- 2000","nGenes \u003c- 100","set.seed(1)","X \u003c- matrix(","  rnbinom(n = nGenes * nCells, size = 20, prob = 0.98),","  ncol = nCells",")","rownames(X) \u003c- c(paste0(\"ng\", 1:90), paste0(\"mt-\", 1:10))","```","","### Generating a perturbed condition","","Genes 10, 2, and 3 are replaced with the expression profiles of genes 50, 11, and 5, respectively.","","```r","Y \u003c- X","Y[10, ] \u003c- Y[50, ]","Y[2, ]  \u003c- Y[11, ]","Y[3, ]  \u003c- Y[5, ]","```","","### Running the pipeline","","Under *H*₀ (no differential regulation) we supply the same matrix for both conditions. Under *H*_A we supply the control and perturbed matrices.","","```r","outputH0 \u003c- scTenifoldNet(X = X, Y = X,","                          nc_nNet = 10, nc_nCells = 500,","                          td_K = 3, qc_minLibSize = 30)","","outputHA \u003c- scTenifoldNet(X = X, Y = Y,","                          nc_nNet = 10, nc_nCells = 500,","                          td_K = 3, qc_minLibSize = 30)","```","","### Inspecting the tensor networks","","The denoised networks are stored as sparse matrices that can be converted to [igraph](https://igraph.org/r/) objects for downstream topological analysis:","","```r","igraph::graph_from_adjacency_matrix(outputHA$tensorNetworks$X, weighted = TRUE)","igraph::graph_from_adjacency_matrix(outputHA$tensorNetworks$Y, weighted = TRUE)","```","","### Differential regulation results","","Under *H*₀, no genes reach significance (FDR \u003c 0.1). Under *H*_A, the six genes involved in the perturbation are correctly identified:","","```r","head(outputH0$diffRegulation, n = 6)","#    gene     distance        Z       FC    p.value     p.adj","# 59 ng59 1.138659e-15 2.497859 4.338493 0.03725989 0.6411916","# 32 ng32 9.970451e-16 2.081719 3.326448 0.06817394 0.6411916","# 72 ng72 9.452170e-16 1.917581 2.989608 0.08380044 0.6411916","# 89 ng89 8.924023e-16 1.742758 2.664849 0.10258758 0.6411916","# 12 ng12 8.851226e-16 1.718018 2.621550 0.10542145 0.6411916","# 17 ng17 8.784453e-16 1.695183 2.582145 0.10807510 0.6411916","","head(outputHA$diffRegulation, n = 6)","#    gene   distance        Z        FC      p.value      p.adj","# 2   ng2 0.023526702 2.762449 12.193413 0.0004795855 0.02414332","# 50 ng50 0.023514429 2.761550 12.180695 0.0004828665 0.02414332","# 11 ng11 0.022443941 2.681598 11.096894 0.0008647241 0.02882414","# 3   ng3 0.020263415 2.508478  9.045415 0.0026335445 0.06583861","# 10 ng10 0.019194561 2.417929  8.116328 0.0043868326 0.07711821","# 5   ng5 0.019079975 2.407977  8.019712 0.0046270923 0.07711821","```","","### Visualizing the results","","Quantile-quantile plots provide a clear summary. Genes with FDR \u003c 0.1 are highlighted in red.","","![QQ-plot example](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/cailab-tamu/scTenifoldNet/master/inst/readmeExample.png)","","```r","par(mfrow = c(2, 1), mar = c(3, 3, 1, 1), mgp = c(1.5, 0.5, 0))","set.seed(1)","qChisq \u003c- rchisq(100, 1)","","geneColor \u003c- rev(ifelse(outputH0$diffRegulation$p.adj \u003c 0.1, \"red\", \"black\"))","qqplot(qChisq, outputH0$diffRegulation$FC, pch = 16, main = expression(H[0]),","       col = geneColor, xlab = expression(chi^2 ~ Quantiles), ylab = \"FC\",","       xlim = c(0, 8), ylim = c(0, 13))","qqline(qChisq)","legend(\"bottomright\", legend = \"FDR \u003c 0.1\", pch = 16, col = \"red\", bty = \"n\", cex = 0.7)","","geneColor \u003c- rev(ifelse(outputHA$diffRegulation$p.adj \u003c 0.1, \"red\", \"black\"))","qqplot(qChisq, outputHA$diffRegulation$FC, pch = 16, main = expression(H[A]),","       col = geneColor, xlab = expression(chi^2 ~ Quantiles), ylab = \"FC\",","       xlim = c(0, 8), ylim = c(0, 13))","qqline(qChisq)","legend(\"bottomright\", legend = \"FDR \u003c 0.1\", pch = 16, col = \"red\", bty = \"n\", cex = 0.7)","```","","## Citation","","If you use **scTenifoldNet** in your research, please cite:","","\u003e Osorio, D., Zhong, Y., Li, G., Huang, J. Z., \u0026 Cai, J. J. (2020). scTenifoldNet: A Machine Learning Workflow for Constructing and Comparing Transcriptome-wide Gene Regulatory Networks from Single-Cell Data. *Patterns*, **1**(9), 100139. [doi:10.1016/j.patter.2020.100139](https://doi.org/10.1016/j.patter.2020.100139)","","BibTeX:","","```bibtex","@Article{osorio2020sctenifoldnet,","  title   = {scTenifoldNet: A Machine Learning Workflow for Constructing and","             Comparing Transcriptome-wide Gene Regulatory Networks from","             Single-Cell Data},","  author  = {Daniel Osorio and Yan Zhong and Guanxun Li and Jianhua Z. Huang","             and James J. Cai},","  journal = {Patterns},","  year    = {2020},","  volume  = {1},","  number  = {9},","  pages   = {100139},","  issn    = {2666-3899},","  doi     = {10.1016/j.patter.2020.100139},","}","```","","---","","\u0026copy; The Texas A\u0026M University System. class="BlobViewContent-module__blobContentWrapper__JS0W6"><section aria-labelledby="file-name-id-wide file-name-id-mobile" class="BlobContent-module__blobContentSection__VOgZq BlobContent-module__blobContentSectionMarkdown__mPLOK" style="margin-top:46px"><div class="js-snippet-clipboard-copy-unpositioned BlobContent-module__markdownBlob__T8jpG" data-hpc="true"><article class="markdown-body entry-content container-lg" itemprop="text"><div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h1 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">scTenifoldNet</h1><a id="user-content-sctenifoldnet" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: scTenifoldNet" href="#sctenifoldnet"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://CRAN.R-project.org/package=scTenifoldNet" rel="nofollow"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/428c95c38b5c762cd95d6d00c3c4ee0a35009db5930bfd73281e6ea13cf88220/68747470733a2f2f7777772e722d706b672e6f72672f6261646765732f76657273696f6e2f736354656e69666f6c644e6574" alt="CRAN" data-canonical-src="https://www.r-pkg.org/badges/version/scTenifoldNet" style="max-width: 100%;"></a>
<a href="https://www.gnu.org/licenses/old-licenses/gpl-2.0.en.html" rel="nofollow"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/c6a371d5595af12d2621de9485b2c112e711b36f75d4073faa7815247469f4c5/68747470733a2f2f696d672e736869656c64732e696f2f62616467652f4c6963656e73652d47504c253230253238253345253344322532392d626c75652e737667" alt="License: GPL (&gt;=2)" data-canonical-src="https://img.shields.io/badge/License-GPL%20%28%3E%3D2%29-blue.svg" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>scTenifoldNet</strong> is an R package for constructing and comparing single-cell gene regulatory networks (scGRNs) from single-cell RNA-seq (scRNA-seq) data collected under different conditions. It employs a machine-learning workflow combining principal component regression, tensor decomposition, and manifold alignment to accurately identify even subtly shifted gene expression programs.</p>
<p dir="auto">Implementations in other languages are also available:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Python</strong>: <a href="https://github.com/qwerty239qwe/scTenifoldpy">scTenifoldpy</a></li>
<li><strong>MATLAB</strong>: <a href="https://github.com/jamesjcai/scGEAToolbox">scGEAToolbox</a></li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Installation</h2><a id="user-content-installation" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Installation" href="#installation"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>scTenifoldNet</strong> is available on CRAN:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-r notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="install.packages(&quot;scTenifoldNet&quot;)"><pre>install.packages(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>scTenifoldNet<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>)</pre></div>
<p dir="auto">To install the development version from GitHub:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-r notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="# install.packages(&quot;remotes&quot;)
remotes::install_github(&quot;cailab-tamu/scTenifoldNet&quot;)"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> install.packages("remotes")</span>
<span class="pl-e">remotes</span><span class="pl-k">::</span>install_github(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>cailab-tamu/scTenifoldNet<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>)</pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Pipeline Overview</h2><a id="user-content-pipeline-overview" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Pipeline Overview" href="#pipeline-overview"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The <code>scTenifoldNet()</code> function orchestrates a six-step pipeline. Each step reports progress to the console via the <a href="https://cli.r-lib.org/" rel="nofollow">cli</a> package, with sample-level labels (<code>[X]</code> / <code>[Y]</code>) so that operations on each condition are clearly distinguishable.</p>
<markdown-accessiblity-table><table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th align="center">Step</th>
<th align="left">Function</th>
<th align="left">Description</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td align="center">1</td>
<td align="left"><code>scQC</code></td>
<td align="left">Quality control — filters cells by library size, outlier detection, minimum gene expression fraction, and mitochondrial read ratio</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="center">2</td>
<td align="left"><code>cpmNormalization</code></td>
<td align="left">Counts-per-million (CPM) normalization</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="center">3</td>
<td align="left"><code>makeNetworks</code></td>
<td align="left">Constructs gene regulatory networks from subsampled cells using principal component regression (<code>pcNet</code>)</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="center">4</td>
<td align="left"><code>tensorDecomposition</code></td>
<td align="left">CANDECOMP/PARAFAC (CP) tensor decomposition for network denoising</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="center">5</td>
<td align="left"><code>manifoldAlignment</code></td>
<td align="left">Non-linear manifold alignment of the two denoised networks</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="center">6</td>
<td align="left"><code>dRegulation</code></td>
<td align="left">Differential regulation testing via Box-Cox transformation and chi-square statistics</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table></markdown-accessiblity-table>
<p dir="auto">Individual functions are exported and fully documented, allowing users to run or modify any step independently.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Input</h2><a id="user-content-input" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Input" href="#input"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The required input is a <strong>raw counts matrix</strong> with genes as rows and cells (barcodes) as columns. Data should be <em>unnormalized</em> when using the main <code>scTenifoldNet()</code> function. The modular design of the package allows users to substitute custom preprocessing at any step.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Output</h2><a id="user-content-output" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Output" href="#output"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><code>scTenifoldNet()</code> returns a list with three elements:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong><code>tensorNetworks</code></strong> — Weight-averaged denoised gene regulatory networks after CP tensor decomposition, containing:
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>X</code>: The network for sample <em>X</em> (sparse matrix of class <code>dgCMatrix</code>).</li>
<li><code>Y</code>: The network for sample <em>Y</em> (sparse matrix of class <code>dgCMatrix</code>).</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong><code>manifoldAlignment</code></strong> — A data frame of low-dimensional features from the non-linear manifold alignment, with 2 × <em>n</em> genes rows and <em>d</em> columns (default <em>d</em> = 30).</li>
<li><strong><code>diffRegulation</code></strong> — A data frame with six columns:
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>gene</code>: Gene identifier.</li>
<li><code>distance</code>: Euclidean distance between the gene's coordinates in the two conditions.</li>
<li><code>Z</code>: Z-score after Box-Cox power transformation.</li>
<li><code>FC</code>: Fold change with respect to the expectation.</li>
<li><code>p.value</code>: P-value from the chi-square distribution with one degree of freedom.</li>
<li><code>p.adj</code>: Adjusted p-value (Benjamini &amp; Hochberg FDR correction).</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Running Time</h2><a id="user-content-running-time" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Running Time" href="#running-time"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Example</h2><a id="user-content-example" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Example" href="#example"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Simulating a dataset</h3><a id="user-content-simulating-a-dataset" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Simulating a dataset" href="#simulating-a-dataset"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">We create a sparse count matrix of 2,000 cells and 100 genes drawn from a negative binomial distribution (~67 % zeros). The last ten genes are prefixed with <code>mt-</code> to simulate mitochondrial genes.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-r notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="library(scTenifoldNet)

nCells &lt;- 2000
nGenes &lt;- 100
set.seed(1)
X &lt;- matrix(
  rnbinom(n = nGenes * nCells, size = 20, prob = 0.98),
  ncol = nCells
)
rownames(X) &lt;- c(paste0(&quot;ng&quot;, 1:90), paste0(&quot;mt-&quot;, 1:10))"><pre>library(<span class="pl-smi">scTenifoldNet</span>)

<span class="pl-smi">nCells</span> <span class="pl-k">&lt;-</span> <span class="pl-c1">2000</span>
<span class="pl-smi">nGenes</span> <span class="pl-k">&lt;-</span> <span class="pl-c1">100</span>
set.seed(<span class="pl-c1">1</span>)
<span class="pl-smi">X</span> <span class="pl-k">&lt;-</span> <span class="pl-k">matrix</span>(
  rnbinom(<span class="pl-v">n</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">nGenes</span> <span class="pl-k">*</span> <span class="pl-smi">nCells</span>, <span class="pl-v">size</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">20</span>, <span class="pl-v">prob</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">0.98</span>),
  <span class="pl-v">ncol</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">nCells</span>
)
rownames(<span class="pl-smi">X</span>) <span class="pl-k">&lt;-</span> c(paste0(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>ng<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>, <span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-k">:</span><span class="pl-c1">90</span>), paste0(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>mt-<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>, <span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-k">:</span><span class="pl-c1">10</span>))</pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Generating a perturbed condition</h3><a id="user-content-generating-a-perturbed-condition" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Generating a perturbed condition" href="#generating-a-perturbed-condition"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Genes 10, 2, and 3 are replaced with the expression profiles of genes 50, 11, and 5, respectively.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-r notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="Y &lt;- X
Y[10, ] &lt;- Y[50, ]
Y[2, ]  &lt;- Y[11, ]
Y[3, ]  &lt;- Y[5, ]"><pre><span class="pl-smi">Y</span> <span class="pl-k">&lt;-</span> <span class="pl-smi">X</span>
<span class="pl-smi">Y</span>[<span class="pl-c1">10</span>, ] <span class="pl-k">&lt;-</span> <span class="pl-smi">Y</span>[<span class="pl-c1">50</span>, ]
<span class="pl-smi">Y</span>[<span class="pl-c1">2</span>, ]  <span class="pl-k">&lt;-</span> <span class="pl-smi">Y</span>[<span class="pl-c1">11</span>, ]
<span class="pl-smi">Y</span>[<span class="pl-c1">3</span>, ]  <span class="pl-k">&lt;-</span> <span class="pl-smi">Y</span>[<span class="pl-c1">5</span>, ]</pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Running the pipeline</h3><a id="user-content-running-the-pipeline" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Running the pipeline" href="#running-the-pipeline"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Under <em>H</em>₀ (no differential regulation) we supply the same matrix for both conditions. Under <em>H</em>_A we supply the control and perturbed matrices.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-r notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="outputH0 &lt;- scTenifoldNet(X = X, Y = X,
                          nc_nNet = 10, nc_nCells = 500,
                          td_K = 3, qc_minLibSize = 30)

outputHA &lt;- scTenifoldNet(X = X, Y = Y,
                          nc_nNet = 10, nc_nCells = 500,
                          td_K = 3, qc_minLibSize = 30)"><pre><span class="pl-smi">outputH0</span> <span class="pl-k">&lt;-</span> scTenifoldNet(<span class="pl-v">X</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">X</span>, <span class="pl-v">Y</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">X</span>,
                          <span class="pl-v">nc_nNet</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">10</span>, <span class="pl-v">nc_nCells</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">500</span>,
                          <span class="pl-v">td_K</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">3</span>, <span class="pl-v">qc_minLibSize</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">30</span>)

<span class="pl-smi">outputHA</span> <span class="pl-k">&lt;-</span> scTenifoldNet(<span class="pl-v">X</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">X</span>, <span class="pl-v">Y</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">Y</span>,
                          <span class="pl-v">nc_nNet</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">10</span>, <span class="pl-v">nc_nCells</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">500</span>,
                          <span class="pl-v">td_K</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">3</span>, <span class="pl-v">qc_minLibSize</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">30</span>)</pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Inspecting the tensor networks</h3><a id="user-content-inspecting-the-tensor-networks" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Inspecting the tensor networks" href="#inspecting-the-tensor-networks"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The denoised networks are stored as sparse matrices that can be converted to <a href="https://igraph.org/r/" rel="nofollow">igraph</a> objects for downstream topological analysis:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-r notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="igraph::graph_from_adjacency_matrix(outputHA$tensorNetworks$X, weighted = TRUE)

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Differential regulation results</h3><a id="user-content-differential-regulation-results" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Differential regulation results" href="#differential-regulation-results"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Under <em>H</em>₀, no genes reach significance (FDR &lt; 0.1). Under <em>H</em>_A, the six genes involved in the perturbation are correctly identified:</p>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Visualizing the results</h3><a id="user-content-visualizing-the-results" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Visualizing the results" href="#visualizing-the-results"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Quantile-quantile plots provide a clear summary. Genes with FDR &lt; 0.1 are highlighted in red.</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/cailab-tamu/scTenifoldNet/master/inst/readmeExample.png"><img src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/cailab-tamu/scTenifoldNet/master/inst/readmeExample.png" alt="QQ-plot example" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-r notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="par(mfrow = c(2, 1), mar = c(3, 3, 1, 1), mgp = c(1.5, 0.5, 0))
set.seed(1)
qChisq &lt;- rchisq(100, 1)

geneColor &lt;- rev(ifelse(outputH0$diffRegulation$p.adj &lt; 0.1, &quot;red&quot;, &quot;black&quot;))
qqplot(qChisq, outputH0$diffRegulation$FC, pch = 16, main = expression(H[0]),
       col = geneColor, xlab = expression(chi^2 ~ Quantiles), ylab = &quot;FC&quot;,
       xlim = c(0, 8), ylim = c(0, 13))
qqline(qChisq)
legend(&quot;bottomright&quot;, legend = &quot;FDR &lt; 0.1&quot;, pch = 16, col = &quot;red&quot;, bty = &quot;n&quot;, cex = 0.7)

geneColor &lt;- rev(ifelse(outputHA$diffRegulation$p.adj &lt; 0.1, &quot;red&quot;, &quot;black&quot;))
qqplot(qChisq, outputHA$diffRegulation$FC, pch = 16, main = expression(H[A]),
       col = geneColor, xlab = expression(chi^2 ~ Quantiles), ylab = &quot;FC&quot;,
       xlim = c(0, 8), ylim = c(0, 13))
qqline(qChisq)
legend(&quot;bottomright&quot;, legend = &quot;FDR &lt; 0.1&quot;, pch = 16, col = &quot;red&quot;, bty = &quot;n&quot;, cex = 0.7)"><pre>par(<span class="pl-v">mfrow</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> c(<span class="pl-c1">2</span>, <span class="pl-c1">1</span>), <span class="pl-v">mar</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> c(<span class="pl-c1">3</span>, <span class="pl-c1">3</span>, <span class="pl-c1">1</span>, <span class="pl-c1">1</span>), <span class="pl-v">mgp</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> c(<span class="pl-c1">1.5</span>, <span class="pl-c1">0.5</span>, <span class="pl-c1">0</span>))
set.seed(<span class="pl-c1">1</span>)
<span class="pl-smi">qChisq</span> <span class="pl-k">&lt;-</span> rchisq(<span class="pl-c1">100</span>, <span class="pl-c1">1</span>)

<span class="pl-smi">geneColor</span> <span class="pl-k">&lt;-</span> rev(ifelse(<span class="pl-smi">outputH0</span><span class="pl-k">$</span><span class="pl-smi">diffRegulation</span><span class="pl-k">$</span><span class="pl-smi">p.adj</span> <span class="pl-k">&lt;</span> <span class="pl-c1">0.1</span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>red<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>black<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>))
qqplot(<span class="pl-smi">qChisq</span>, <span class="pl-smi">outputH0</span><span class="pl-k">$</span><span class="pl-smi">diffRegulation</span><span class="pl-k">$</span><span class="pl-smi">FC</span>, <span class="pl-v">pch</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">16</span>, <span class="pl-v">main</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> expression(<span class="pl-smi">H</span>[<span class="pl-c1">0</span>]),
       <span class="pl-v">col</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">geneColor</span>, <span class="pl-v">xlab</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> expression(<span class="pl-smi">chi</span><span class="pl-k">^</span><span class="pl-c1">2</span> <span class="pl-k">~</span> <span class="pl-smi">Quantiles</span>), <span class="pl-v">ylab</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>FC<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
       <span class="pl-v">xlim</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> c(<span class="pl-c1">0</span>, <span class="pl-c1">8</span>), <span class="pl-v">ylim</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> c(<span class="pl-c1">0</span>, <span class="pl-c1">13</span>))
qqline(<span class="pl-smi">qChisq</span>)
legend(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>bottomright<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>, <span class="pl-v">legend</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>FDR &lt; 0.1<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>, <span class="pl-v">pch</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">16</span>, <span class="pl-v">col</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>red<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>, <span class="pl-v">bty</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>n<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>, <span class="pl-v">cex</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">0.7</span>)

<span class="pl-smi">geneColor</span> <span class="pl-k">&lt;-</span> rev(ifelse(<span class="pl-smi">outputHA</span><span class="pl-k">$</span><span class="pl-smi">diffRegulation</span><span class="pl-k">$</span><span class="pl-smi">p.adj</span> <span class="pl-k">&lt;</span> <span class="pl-c1">0.1</span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>red<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>black<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>))
qqplot(<span class="pl-smi">qChisq</span>, <span class="pl-smi">outputHA</span><span class="pl-k">$</span><span class="pl-smi">diffRegulation</span><span class="pl-k">$</span><span class="pl-smi">FC</span>, <span class="pl-v">pch</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">16</span>, <span class="pl-v">main</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> expression(<span class="pl-smi">H</span>[<span class="pl-smi">A</span>]),
       <span class="pl-v">col</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">geneColor</span>, <span class="pl-v">xlab</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> expression(<span class="pl-smi">chi</span><span class="pl-k">^</span><span class="pl-c1">2</span> <span class="pl-k">~</span> <span class="pl-smi">Quantiles</span>), <span class="pl-v">ylab</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>FC<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
